📋 HOW TO READ THIS DOCUMENT — NAVIGATION GUIDE 
Purpose 
Audience: GAPLMB Management, Development Team, UAT 
Team 
Finding a Module 
Each module (M-01 to M-10) begins with a MODULE QUICK 
REFERENCE box (teal header). Read that box first — it tells you 
all screens, rules, and use cases in that module without needing to 
read every page. 
Functional 
Requirements 
Section 5.2 (M-02), 6.1 (M-03), 7.1 (M-04) etc. — numbered FR-
[MODULE]-[NNN]. All requirements within each module are 
uniquely identified; numbering is sequential within each module’s 
feature set. 
Data Dictionaries Section 5.5 (M-02 data), 6.2 (M-03 data) etc. Screen Descriptions 
reference the exact dictionary section (e.g., "fields defined in 
§5.5.0") so you do not need to search. 
Use Cases Each use case is fully self-contained: it embeds the relevant 
business rules, screen name, error codes, and actor steps inline — 
no page-turning required. 
Error Codes Error codes (E-AST-001, E-PRE-001 etc.) are defined in the Error 
Handling section of each module. Each use case also lists the 
relevant error codes inline. 
Business Rules Business rules (BR-xxx-NN) appear inline inside the Functional 
Requirements table for each FR. Key rules are also repeated inside 
relevant use cases so developers see rules and workflow in one 
place. 
Design Decisions Section 18 documents the design decisions that govern this SRS and 
must be observed during implementation.

1. Introduction 
1.1 Purpose 
 
This Software Requirements Specification (SRS) defines the complete, agreed requirements for 
the Integrated Online Management System (IOMS) developed for the Goa Agricultural Produce 
and Livestock Marketing Board (GAPLMB). This document is intended for GAPLMB 
management, the development team, the testing/UAT team, and project auditors. It covers all 10 
functional modules, the three -tier approval workflow (DO→DV→DA), non -functional 
requirements, system architecture, and data requirements. 
 
Key purposes of this document: 
• Provide the complete, authoritative requirements baseline for client review and approval. 
• Define all business rules. All rules in this document are binding. 
• Serve as the foundation for development and UAT planning. 
• Document the Employee–User ID coupling rule governing all system access. 
• Define the mobile-first PWA architecture enabling future native app development (see §2.1, 
§14.4). 
 
Requirement Identification Convention:  
• Functional requirements follow the format FR-[MODULE]-[NNN] (e.g., FR -EMP-001, 
FR-AST-001).  
• Business rules follow BR-[MODULE]-[NN].  
• Error codes follow E-[MODULE]-[NNN].  
• Non-functional requirements follow NFR-[CATEGORY]-[NN] (e.g., NFR -PERF-01, 
NFR-AVAIL-01).  
• Use cases follow UC-[MODULE]-[NN] (e.g., UC-EMP-01).

• All identifiers are unique within the document and are used as the primary reference keys in 
the Requirements Traceability Matrix (§19.3 Appendix C — RTM).

1.2 Scope 
 
The GAPLMB IOMS is a centralised, web-based enterprise application hosted on a 
Government-approved Public Cloud (AWS), serving the Head Office, 8 Market Sub-Yards, 
and 5 Border Check Posts.

1.4 Critical Design Principle — Employee–User ID Coupling 
 
⚡ CRITICAL DESIGN RULE: Employee–User ID Coupling  A User ID can only be 
created when a corresponding Employee record with Status = Active exists in M-01. The User 
ID is permanently and immutably linked to the Employee ID. When an employee becomes 
Inactive, Retired, Suspended, or Resigned, the linked User ID is automatically 
disabled in the same database transaction. No User ID can exist without a valid active 
Employee record. This constraint is enforced at both the database level 
(referential integrity) and the application level.

GAPLMB IOMS is a new system with no direct predecessor. It replaces manual, 
paper-based, and fragmented spreadsheet -based processes currently in use across 
GAPLMB Head Office, 8 Sub -Yards, and 5 Border Check Posts . All 10 modules 
share a common Employee/User master , a common three -tier approval workflow 
engine (DO→DV→DA) , and a centralised notification service. The system is 
architected as a mobile -first Progressive Web App (PWA). Future native mobile apps 
require only a native shell; all backend APIs, business logic, and data models remain 
unchanged. 
 
  

--- PAGE 20 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 20 of 435 
2. System Overview 
2.1 Product Perspective 
The GAPLMB Integrated Online Management System (IOMS) is a new, standalone, centralised 
web-based enterprise application. It does not replace or interface with any prior computerised 
system; it replaces manual, paper -based, and fragmented spreadsheet -based processes currently 
in use across GAPLMB Head Office, 8 Sub -Yards, and 5 Border Check Posts. The IOMS is not 
a component of a larger system family and has no predecessor system from which data 
migration is required. 
The system is architected as a Mobile -First Progressive Web App (PWA) hosted on a 
Government-approved Public Cloud (AWS), accessible via standard browsers on desktop and 
mobile devices without requiring a dedicated client installation. All 10 functional modules (M -
01 to M -10) share a common Employee/User master (M -01), a common three -tier approval 
workflow engine (DO→DV→DA), and a centralised notification service. The REST/JSON API 
layer is versioned and designed from the outset to support future native mobile applications 
(React Native / Flutter) without structural change to the backend (see §14.4, §15.1).

Aspect Specification 
Cloud Hosting Government-approved Public Cloud (AWS). Hosted on 
Government-approved infrastructure with DR at a secondary 
NIC/SDC location. 
Supported Browsers Chrome, Firefox, Edge, and Safari — latest 2 major versions. 
Mobile-responsive PWA. 
Min. Client Hardware 1366 x 768 screen resolution; 4 Mbps internet connection. 
Offline / Connectivity Intermittent connectivity at Border Check Posts: offline-graceful 
design with local queuing and auto-sync on reconnect. 
Mobile Devices Android 11+ or iOS 16+ for PWA. Future native app (React 
Native / Flutter) uses same backend API without change (see 
§14.4, §15.1). 
System Constraints 
(Summary — see §17.1 
for full details) 
Description 
GST Compliance All GST invoice generation, tax calculations, return data, and 
TDS processing shall conform to current GSTN specifications 
and applicable Indian tax law. 
Aadhaar Data Protection The system shall capture and store Aadhaar data exclusively in 
masked format (XXXX-XXXX-1234). No unmasked Aadhaar 
value shall be stored, displayed, processed, transmitted, or logged 
at any stage. 
Source Code All source code shall be maintained in a Government-approved 
version control repository (NIC GitLab or equivalent). 
Technology Stack React.js/Angular for frontend; PostgreSQL/MySQL for database 
(Government-approved). Deviations require prior written

--- PAGE 25 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 25 of 435 
Entity ID / Premises ID / Entity:  
• "Entity ID" — global internal system key assigned to every entity in M-02 (format: 
ENT-[YYYY]-[NNNNN]; organisation-wide unique, location-independent, immutable). 
For Track A entities, the user-facing identifier is the Licence Number; for Track B 
entities (all sub-types including Ad-hoc Occupant), the Entity ID is also the user-facing 
identifier. Searches may be performed by Entity Name (all tracks) or Licence Number 
(Track A) / Entity ID (Track B).  
• "Premises ID" — unique identifier per physical premises unit (format: [YARD-CODE]-
[TYPE-CODE]-[NNNN]; unique system-wide).  
• A single Entity may hold one or more Premises IDs (one-to-many). 
•  All three categories are collectively called "Entity".  
• All API field names and database columns shall use "Entity ID", and "Premises ID" as 
authoritative terms. 
 
Tapal / Dak:  
• In M-09 (Correspondence Management), "Tapal" is the authoritative term for all 
official paper-based correspondence (letters, notices, and official communications) 
received or dispatched by GAPLMB.  
• "Dak" is a recognised colloquial synonym acceptable in legacy documents and printed 
registers, but all system fields, screen labels, API field names, and database columns 
shall use "Tapal". 
• Inward Tapal reference format: IN-[LOC]-[YYYY]-[NNNNN].  
• Outward Tapal reference format: OUT-[LOC]-[YYYY]-[NNNNN]. 
 
Track A / Track B:  
• Within M-02, entities are classified as follows: 
o  Track A (Market Functionaries — Trader Holding APMC licence and subject 
to Market Fee) or Track B (Government Departments, PSUs, and Institutional 
Entities occupying GAPLMB premises for non-trading purposes, exempt from 
Market Fee).  
o Full classification, sub-types, and GST treatment are defined in §5 (M-02).

3.2 Workflow Business Rules 
Rule ID Business Rule Description 
BR-WF-01 The same user cannot act as more than one of DO, DV, or DA for the same 
record. 
BR-WF-02 A record in Submitted state cannot be edited by the DO until it is Returned 
by the DV. 
BR-WF-03 Rejection by DA is mandatory with a Rejection Reason Code (from a 
configurable list) plus free-text remarks of minimum 10 characters. 
BR-WF-04 A Rejected record returns to Draft state; the DO may revise and resubmit. 
Revision count is tracked. 
BR-WF-05 Escalation SLA thresholds are configurable per module by the System 
Administrator. Default: DV SLA = 3 working days; DA SLA = 5 working 
days. 
BR-WF-06 All workflow stage transitions are logged in the audit trail with actor, 
timestamp, IP address, and remarks.

4. M-01: HRMS and Service Record Management 
 
M-01 MODULE QUICK REFERENCE — HRMS and Service Record Management 
Purpose 
Manage the complete employee lifecycle: registration, leave, 
TA/DA, LTC, and system configuration.  
All staff records that underpin RBAC user accounts live here. 
User Roles 
DO: HR staff (creates records). DV: HR Supervisor (verifies). 
DA: HR Manager / Secretary (approves). Auditor: read-only. 
Functional Requirements • FR-EMP-001: Employee Registration 
• FR-EMP-002: Aadhaar Capture (Masked) 
• FR-EMP-003: Document Management 
• FR-EMP-004: Service Book 
• FR-EMP-005: Status Management and Retirement 
• FR-LVE-001 to FR-LVE-003: Leave types. 
• FR-TADA-001 to FR-TADA-004: TA/DA. 
• FR-LTC-001 to FR-LTC-004: LTC. 
• FR-CFG-001 to FR-CFG-003: Config. Full rules: §4.1 
Screens SCR-EMP-01 to SCR-EMP-05: Employee module screens. 
Full descriptions: §4.1.2 
Data Dictionaries • §4.1 Employee Master 
• §4.2 Leave Management 
• §4.3 TA/DA 
• §4.4 Configuration 
• §4.5 LTC 
Use Cases UC-EMP-01: New Employee Registration. 
 Full use cases: §4.1.3

account) 
• M-06 (TA/DA claims generate payment vouchers). 
This module is the master data source for all employees of GAPLMB. Every User ID in the 
system is derived from an active Employee record in this module. Configuration of all system -
wide parameters (pay rates, TA/DA rates, leave rules, LTC rules) is also managed through 
this module.

checks against all stored

4.3 TA/DA — Travelling Allowance and Daily Allowance 
 
Terminology note: In this section, "DA" refers to Daily Allowance (a travel entitlement). 
Where the document refers to the Data Approver (the Secretary), the full term "DA 
(Secretary)" or "Data Approver" is used. These are distinct concepts and should not be 
confused.

4.5 Leave Travel Concession (LTC) Management 
 
Leave Travel Concession (LTC) is a statutory entitlement for GAPLMB employees under 
Government of Goa service rules. The system manages LTC application, tour plan approval, bill 
submission, leave encashment linkage, and reimbursement workflow. All values are 
configurable by the Configuration Manager. 
 
4.5.1 LTC Functional Requirements

and type (Home Town / All-India)

(configurable).

per block period per employee.

specify advance LTC leave applied

5. M-02: Trader and Entity Management 
5.1 Module Overview 
 
M-02 MODULE QUICK REFERENCE — Entity ID, Entity Profile and 
Premises Management 
Purpose 
Register every ENTITY (Trader, Non-Trader, or Ad-hoc Occupant) 
occupying GAPLMB premises.  
Assign Entity IDs (Licence Number displayed for Track A; Entity ID 
for Track B), manage premises allocations, and maintain the physical 
Premises Master (M-02-PM).  
Three entity types:  
Track A (Traders),  
Track B (Non-Traders: Govt, Commercial), and  
Ad-hoc Occupants (Track B sub-type). 
User Roles 
DO — Data Originator (Yard Officer): creates records.  
DV — Data Verifier: reviews and verifies.  
DA — Data Approver (Secretary): approves, can override. 
 Auditor: read-only access to all records. 
Functional

M-02 manages the full lifecycle of every ENTITY that occupies or uses 
GAPLMB-owned premises. The module recognises two distinct occupant tracks, 
each with its own registration workflow, licence obligations, GST treatment, and 
billing rules. 
 
Track Who Qualifies Key Characteristics 
Track A 
Market 
Functionary / 
Trader 
Individual, Proprietary Firm, 
Partnership, Company, Co-
operative, HUF, NGO, 
Government Undertaking — 
trading or processing 
agricultural produce within a 
GAPLMB yard or outside 
Yard but is a Licence Holder 
for the State of Goa. 
• Must hold a valid GAPLMB 
Registration Certificate under Section 
53(3) of the Goa APMRD Act 2007. 
• Licence Categories/Type:  
o A Class Trader 
o B Class Trader 
o C Class Trader 
o Assistant to Trader 
•  They are subject to Market Fee. 
• GST on rent as applicable. 
• Can hold premises in one or multiple 
yards under a single profile. 
Track B Non-
Trader Lease 
Holder 
Government Department / 
Office, Government 
Undertaking / PSU, 
Nationalised or Scheduled 
Bank, Commercial 
Institution / Corporate 
Office, Canteen / Food 
Vendor — occupying 
GAPLMB premises for non-
trading operational purposes. 
• No Trader Licence required. 
• Not subject to Market Fee. 
• Monthly rental basis only. 
• GST applicability is sub-type-dependent: 
o  Government entities — GST 
EXEMPT (zero-rated); 
o all others — GST applicable at 
prevailing rate. 
• Government entities receive a Pre-
Receipt (Demand Note) for 
departmental budget settlement instead 
of a standard tax invoice.

5.2.1 Ad-hoc Occupant (Track B) — Functional Requirements 
An Ad-hoc Occupant is an entity occupying GAPLMB premises without a formally 
classified Track B sub-type. Ad-hoc Occupants are not subject to Market Fee (M-04) and do not 
hold a trader licence. They follow the standard Track B registration workflow (DO→DV→DA), 
receive a global Entity ID (format: ENT-[YYYY]-[NNNNN]) on DA approval, and are subject 
to configurable GST per entity at the Premises Allocation Record level. The following 
requirements govern Ad-hoc Occupant registration and tenancy management. 
 
 — Ad-hoc Occupant Registration and Entity ID Generation (Track B) 
FR-NRT-001 — Ad-hoc Occupant Registration and Entity ID Generation (Track B): The 
system shall allow a DO to register an Ad-hoc Occupant as a Track B entity in M-02. On 
DA approval, the system shall auto-generate a global Entity ID in the format ENT-
[YYYY]-[NNNNN]. The Entity ID is organisation-wide unique, location-independent, and 
immutable once assigned. Business Rules: BR-NRT-01: Entity ID generated at DA 
approval; no manual entry permitted. BR-NRT-02: Entity ID cannot be re-used or 
transferred. BR-NRT-03: An Ad-hoc Occupant record must capture at minimum: Entity 
Name, Contact Mobile, Contact Address, and the Premises ID(s) to be occupied. BR-NRT-
04: PAN is mandatory if annual rent exceeds the TDS threshold (configurable per BR-
RENT-15). BR-NRT-05: Ad-hoc Occupant records follow the standard Track B DO → 
DV → DA three-tier approval workflow. Priority: Critical. Track: B. 
FR-NRT-003 — Ad-hoc Occupant Tenancy Record Management (Track B): The system 
shall maintain a complete, permanent tenancy history for each Ad-hoc Occupant, linked 
to their Entity ID. The tenancy record shall include: all Premises IDs occupied (current 

--- PAGE 103 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 103 of 435 
and historical), agreement dates, rent amounts, payment receipts, and any outstanding 
dues. Business Rule: BR-NRT-12: Rent invoicing for Ad-hoc Occupants follows the 
standard Track B M-03 workflow; GST applicability is configurable per entity at the 
Premises Allocation Record level. Note — All other tenancy behaviours (read-only 
closure, permanent history, ageing-bucket dues tracking, dues blocking new allocation) 
are governed by FR-AST-001, FR-AST-005, FR-AST-006, and FR-AST-010, which apply 
equally to all Track B sub-types. Priority: Critical. Track: B.

The following additional sub-type is recognised under Track B: 
Ad-hoc Occupant (Track B sub-type): An entity occupying GAPLMB premises without a 
formally classified Track B sub-type. Ad-hoc Occupants are not subject to Market Fee (M-04) 
and do not hold a trader licence. GST applicability is configurable per entity at the Premises 
Allocation Record level. The system generates a global Entity ID (format: ENT-[YYYY]-
[NNNNN]) on DA approval — this ID is organisation-wide unique and location-independent. 
Ad-hoc Occupants follow the standard Track B DO → DV → DA workflow and may hold 
premises across multiple yards simultaneously under the same Entity ID.

SCR-TRD-04 — Outstanding Dues and Payment Screen (Self-Service Portal + 
Counter) 
Purpose 
Enables an entity holder to view outstanding dues across all premises 
and initiate payment online or at the counter. 
Actor(s) 
Entity Holder (via self-service portal); 
 DO / Receipt Officer (at counter on entity's behalf) 
Dues Panel 
Summary cards: Total Outstanding (₹) | Current Month Due (₹) | 
Overdue (₹) | Security Deposit Held (₹). Detail grid: per-premises × 
per-month with invoice number, amount, due date, status. 
Payment Options 
— Online 
[Pay Selected] — entity selects one or more invoices  
[Pay All Outstanding] — single gateway transaction.  
Payment modes: UPI | Net Banking | Credit Card | Debit Card. 
Gateway response triggers M-05 receipt. 
Payment Options 
— Counter 
Counter staff selects entity, chooses invoices to settle, records Cash / 
Cheque / DD / NEFT. [Generate Counter Receipt] triggers M-05 
receipt workflow. 
Track B Govt. 
Entities 
Online payment button hidden. Screen shows Pre-Receipt download, 
department contact, and [Mark as Settled] action (DA-only, after 
receiving NEFT/cheque confirmation). 
Post-Payment 
Ledger updated in real-time. SMS and Email receipt dispatched. Dues 
panel refreshed. If cheque: status = Provisional until bank clearance 
confirmed.

5.5.2 Premises Allocation Record (One per Premises per Entity) 
Each Premises Allocation Record captures the contractual and financial terms that govern one 
entity’s occupation of one GAPLMB premises unit. A single entity may hold multiple Premises 
Allocation Records simultaneously (one per premises, across one or multiple yards), all linked 
to the same Entity ID. Each record is independently managed and independently billable. 

--- PAGE 124 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 124 of 435 
Physical premises attributes — Premises Name, Yard, Type, Area, and Dimensions — are not 
re-entered on this record. They are retrieved at run-time via a mandatory foreign-key reference 
to the Premises Master (§5.5.0, field: Premises ID FK). This design eliminates data duplication, 
ensures a single source of truth for physical premises data, and means that any authorised 
update to the Premises Master is automatically reflected on all active and historical allocation 
records without requiring manual correction. Edge cases and data-integrity safeguards are 
documented in the Annotations section below. 
 
Key Relationships:  
Premises Allocation Record —— Premises ID (FK) ——→ Premises Master (§5.5.0)  
Premises Allocation Record —— Entity ID (FK) ——→ Entity Master (§5.5.1) 
Premises Charge Lines (§5.5.3) —— Premises Ref. No. (FK) ——→ Premises Allocation

⚠ Annotations — FK Design: Edge Cases and Data-Integrity Safeguards 
EC-01 | Updating a Premises Master entry after allocation is approved: Physical attribute 
changes in §5.5.0 (e.g. correcting Area or Premises Name) are immediately reflected on all 
Allocation Records that FK-reference that Premises ID. Safeguard: changes to §5.5.0 require 
DA approval (FR-PRE-002, BR-PRE-011/013). The Audit Trail records the before/after 
values with timestamp and approver identity. Active invoices are not retroactively altered; the 
changed value applies from the next billing cycle. 
EC-02 | Premises declared Unsafe for Occupation or Demolished: Once a Premises Master 
record transitions to Unsafe or Demolished, its Premises ID is frozen. No new Premises 
Allocation Records may be created against it (BR-PRE-012). Existing active allocations must 
be terminated by the DO under DA supervision. Historical allocation records remain 
permanently readable for audit (BR-PRE-014). 
EC-03 | Cascading deletion is prohibited: The Premises Allocation Record is never 
physically deleted, even after vacation (Allocation Status = Vacated). The FK to Premises 
Master must not be implemented as a CASCADE DELETE constraint. Implement as 
RESTRICT (or NO ACTION) at the database level: deletion of a Premises Master record must 
be blocked if any Allocation Record (active or historical) references it. 
EC-04 | Changing the Yard or Premises Type on the Master after allocation: These fields 
drive the Premises ID prefix and the type-code, both of which are immutable after initial DA 
approval (BR-PRE-005). A Yard or Type correction therefore requires creating a new 
Premises Master record with the correct values and migrating the allocation via a formal DA-
approved Change Request. The old Premises ID is retired (status = Demolished or 
superseded). This constraint protects the integrity of all historical invoices that reference the 
old Premises ID. 
EC-05 | Multiple active allocations per Premises ID are blocked: The system enforces that 
at most one Allocation Record per Premises ID may have Allocation Status = Active at any 
time (BR-PRE-023). Database implementation: add a partial unique index on (Premises_ID, 
Allocation_Status) where Allocation_Status = 'Active'. 

--- PAGE 139 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 139 of 435 
EC-06 | Read-only derived fields in the UI: Premises Name, Yard / Location, and Premises 
Type must be rendered as read-only, system-populated fields in all allocation entry screens 
(SCR-TRD-02, SCR-TRD-05). The DO selects a Premises ID from the Premises Directory 
(SCR-PRE-01); the system immediately auto-populates all derived fields via the FK lookup. 
No freetext entry of these fields is permitted. 
EC-07 | Rent Revision Mode is set at first allotment and cannot be changed without DA 
override and a mandatory audit trail entry (BR-AST-80). If a certificate entity later loses PWD 
Certificate applicability (e.g. entity type changes), the DA must explicitly switch the mode to 
Standard via a Change Request, record the effective date, and update the Allocation Audit 
History. The switch takes effect from the next renewal cycle — not mid-agreement. 
EC-08 | Break in occupancy resets the Consecutive Renewal Count. If a Standard-mode 
entity vacates and is later re-allotted the same or a different premises, the count restarts from 
0. The system detects a break when a new Premises Allocation Record is created for an entity 
whose prior allocation for the same premises has Status = Vacated. No carry-over of prior 
renewal count is permitted (BR-AST-81). 
EC-09 | PWD Certificate amount mismatch. If the DO enters a PWD Certified Rent that 
differs from the amount stated on the uploaded certificate PDF, DV must flag the discrepancy 
during verification. DA cannot approve until the DO corrects the entry to match the certificate. 
System cross-validation is advisory (amount check against prior period); the uploaded 
certificate PDF is the authoritative source. 
EC-10 | Partial-period rent revision (mid-agreement). Rent revision applies only at the start 
of a renewal period — never mid-agreement. If GAPLMB receives a revised PWD Certificate 
mid-agreement, the new amount takes effect at the next renewal date, not immediately. DA 
may not override this rule without issuing a formal Change Request approved by the 
Secretary. 
EC-11 | Standard-path entities beyond the 4th renewal. From the 4th renewal onward, the 
Rent Revision Rate applies at every subsequent renewal (not only at the 4th). Each renewal 
compounds on the previously approved revised rent. Example: Base Rent = ₹1,000; Rate = 
10%. 4th renewal: ₹1,100. 5th renewal: ₹1,210. 6th renewal: ₹1,331. The system computes 

--- PAGE 140 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 140 of 435 
each revised rent as: Revised Rent = Most Recent Approved Monthly Rent × (1 + Rate ÷ 100) 
per BR-AST-82. 
 
  

--- PAGE 141 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 141 of 435 
5.5.3 Premises Charge Lines — Non-GST Charges per Premises 
In addition to rent, GAPLMB recovers certain premises-specific charges from occupants. These 
charges — such as Garbage Charges, Verandah Charges, and Open Space Charges — do NOT 
attract GST and are collected separately from the GST-applicable rent. Each charge type is 
defined in the Premises Charge Type Master (managed via M-01 Configuration Console), 
assigned a mandatory Tally ledger head mapping, and allocated per premises at a configurable 
rate. The Premises Charge Line records link a specific charge type to a specific Premises 
Allocation Record. The Premises breakup screen (SCR-TRD-09) shows the occupant the full 
financial picture: Rent + GST + each non-GST charge line as separate rows with their totals and 
a grand total monthly liability.

ID

-001

5.5.5 Licence Fee Rate Matrix (Configurable) 
The following rate matrix applies to new licence issuance and annual renewal under Rule 
71(2)(4) & (7) of the Goa Agricultural Produce Marketing (Regulation and Development) Act 
2007. All amounts are configurable via the M-01 Configuration Console (maker-checker: 
Configuration Manager proposes, DA approves) with effective-date scheduling so that future 
upward revisions mandated by the Government of Goa take effect on the notified date without 
any code change. The matrix is pre-seeded at go-live with the rates provided by GAPLMB.

⚠ Ambiguities, Inconsistencies & Clarification Items 
✓ RESOLVED — AMB-01 | BR-AST-74: DA Override Justification field formalised. A 
mandatory free-text field (minimum 300 characters) has been added to the fee-override 
workflow. The field is mandatory — system blocks submission if empty or below 300 
characters. On DA approval, the justification is permanently linked to the respective M-05 
receipt record and printed on the internal receipt copy. See updated BR-AST-74 
Approval/Workflow and Audit/Notes cells above. 
✓ RESOLVED via AMB-03 decision — AMB-02 | BR-AST-75: Category downgrade is NOT 
permitted during renewal. The system blocks any renewal where the entity record shows a 
lower Category than the previously licenced Category. No fee refund or credit note scenario 
arises since downgrade is blocked before the receipt is generated. See updated BR-AST-75 for 
full upgrade/downgrade logic. 
✓ RESOLVED — AMB-03 | BR-AST-75: Category upgrade during renewal is allowed; 
Category downgrade during renewal is NOT allowed. For an upgrade: the upgraded Category 
must be formally approved in the entity record via the standard DO → DV → DA workflow 
before renewal is processed. For a downgrade: system blocks the renewal; the DO must resolve 
the Category discrepancy with DA approval before renewal can resume. See updated BR-AST-
75 Description, Action, and Approval/Workflow cells above. 
✓ RESOLVED — AMB-04 | BR-AST-76: For Licence Fee Rate Matrix revisions specifically, 
the effective date must be at least 1 full business day after DA approval timestamp, overriding 
the general BR-CFG-10 minimum of 1 hour for this matrix only. System blocks effective dates 
less than 1 business day ahead. On approval, system notifies all yard DOs and DVs by email. 
See updated BR-AST-76 Description and Approval/Workflow cells above. 
✓ RESOLVED — AMB-05 | BR-AST-79: Late fee trigger is now precisely defined in FR-
AST-014 (§5.5.6) as the Late Fee Effective Date, configurable per Market Year via M-01. Late 
fee is mandatory on all renewal receipts processed on or after this date for licences expired in 
the prior Market Year. See BR-AST-89 for full specification. 
✓ RESOLVED — AMB-06 | BR-AST-79: Late fee waiver workflow is now fully specified in 

--- PAGE 156 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 156 of 435 
BR-AST-93 (§5.5.6). DO raises waiver request with mandatory justification (≥ 300 chars); DV 
forwards to DA; DA approves (waiver applied, Late Fee = ₹0) or rejects with mandatory 
Rejection Reason Code. All outcomes permanently logged in receipt audit trail and M-02 entity 
history. 
AMB-07 | General — Rule 71(2)(4) & (7) citation: The Rule reference should be verified 
against the current Goa APMRD Act 2007 as amended. If subordinate rules or bye-laws have 
been updated since the Act's original publication, the citation in BR-AST-78 and in the receipt 
template must be updated accordingly. GAPLMB legal team should confirm the current 
applicable rule number before go-live. 
5.5.6 Licence Expiry, Late Fee and Renewal Transaction Rules 
This section defines the system-ready specification for all rules governing licence expiry, the 
transaction validity window, late fee calculation, and renewal cutoff logic for Track A Market 
Functionaries. All configurable parameters are managed exclusively through the M-01 
Configuration Console (Configuration Manager maker / DA approver) and take effect without 
any code deployment. The rules defined here apply at every Yard and Border Check Post and 
are automatically linked at the point of each licence transaction. 
 
FR-AST-014: Market Year — Licence Expiry — Transaction Window Linkage 
FR-AST-014 — Licence Expiry, Late Fee and Renewal Transaction Rules: The system shall 
automatically link, for every Track A licence transaction at any Yard or Border Check Post, the 
following four fields: (1) Market Year (derived from the transaction date against the configured 
Market Year Master), (2) Licence Expiry Date (from the entity licence record in M-02), (3) 
Transaction Window End Date (configurable per Market Year — the last date on which an 
expired licence may still be used for Market Fee transactions at yards and check posts), and (4) 
Late Fee Calculation (auto-computed based on the configurable Late Fee Effective Date and 
Late Fee Amount). These four fields shall be computed dynamically at run-time for every 
transaction and shall reflect the latest approved configuration without any code change. Priority: 
Critical. Track: A.

Logic Flow: Licence Expiry → Transaction → Late Fee → Renewal Cutoff 
Logic Flow: Licence Expiry → Transaction Availability → Late Fee → Renewal Cutoff 
PHASE 1 — TRANSACTION ATTEMPT 
Step 
1 
DO initiates a Market Fee transaction at a Yard or Border Check Post. 
Step 
2 
System auto-derives Market Year from transaction date using the Market Year 
Master. 
Step 
3 
System looks up Licence Expiry Date from the entity's active licence record in M-02. 
Step 
4 
System compares transaction date against three thresholds (all configurable per 
Market Year): • Is transaction date ≤ Licence Expiry Date? → Status: ACTIVE (go to 
Step 5a). • Is transaction date > Licence Expiry Date AND ≤ Transaction Window 
End Date? → Status: GRACE WINDOW (go to Step 5b). • Is transaction date > 
Transaction Window End Date? → Status: HARD-BLOCKED (go to Step 5c). 
Step 
5a 
ACTIVE: Transaction proceeds normally. No warning. No late fee on transaction. 
Renewal reminders still dispatched per BR-AST-94 schedule if expiry is approaching. 
Step 
5b 
GRACE WINDOW: Transaction proceeds. System displays mandatory on-screen 
warning: "Licence expired on [DATE]. Renewal required before [Transaction 
Window End Date]." Transaction is flagged "Grace Period Transaction" in M-04 and 
M-05. Renewal prompt (POP + SMS + Email) auto-generated to DO and entity 
holder. 
Step 
5c 
HARD-BLOCKED: Transaction rejected. Error E-AST-002 displayed. DO is directed 
to M-02 to initiate renewal. No transaction accepted until renewal is approved or DA 
post-cutoff override is granted. 
PHASE 2 — RENEWAL PROCESSING 
Step 
6 
DO opens the Renewal screen for the expired licence. System checks the current date 
against: • Is current date < Late Fee Effective Date? → Standard Renewal (go to Step 

--- PAGE 177 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 177 of 435 
7a). • Is current date ≥ Late Fee Effective Date AND ≤ Renewal Cutoff Date? → Late 
Renewal (go to Step 7b). • Is current date > Renewal Cutoff Date? → Post-Cutoff: 
DA Override Required (go to Step 7c). 
Step 
7a 
STANDARD RENEWAL: Base Licence Fee applied. No Late Fee. Renewal follows 
standard DO → DV → DA workflow. Receipt generated with Renewal Type = 
"Standard". 
Step 
7b 
LATE RENEWAL: System auto-computes Late Fee per configured mode (Flat or 
Percentage). Late Fee appended as mandatory non-removable line item on receipt. DO 
cannot remove Late Fee without DA waiver (BR-AST-93). Renewal follows DO → 
DV → DA workflow. Receipt generated with Renewal Type = "Late". 
Step 
7c 
POST-CUTOFF: System blocks renewal. Error message displayed with Renewal 
Cutoff Date. A DA Override Request is auto-created and routed to DA. DA reviews, 
approves (with ≥ 300-char justification) or rejects. If approved: Late Fee applied, 
renewal processed, receipt generated with Renewal Type = "Post-Cutoff-DA-
Approved" and "Secretary-Authorised" watermark. 
PHASE 3 — LATE FEE CALCULATION 
Step 
8 
System retrieves Late Fee Calculation Mode from M-01 configuration: • Mode = 
FLAT: Late Fee = configured fixed amount (e.g. ₹50). • Mode = PERCENTAGE: 
Late Fee = Base Licence Fee × (Configured Rate ÷ 100). Result is rounded to the 
nearest rupee. Both the mode and result are shown on the renewal screen before the 
DO submits. 
Step 
9 
Late Fee is written as a named line item "Late Renewal Fee" on the M-05 receipt. 
Base Licence Fee row in the Licence Fee Rate Matrix is unchanged. Receipt total = 
Base Licence Fee + Late Fee (+ GST if applicable). 
Step 
10 
If DA Waiver requested (BR-AST-93): waiver workflow runs in parallel. Receipt is 
held in "Pending Waiver Decision" state. On DA decision: receipt finalised with 
either Late Fee or ₹0 waiver applied. 
PHASE 4 — POST-RENEWAL 

--- PAGE 178 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 178 of 435 
Step 
11 
On DA approval of renewal: new Licence Expiry Date (31 March of next Market 
Year) is set on the entity record. Licence Status returns to "Active". Hard-Block (if 
applied) is automatically lifted. Entity visibility restored across all Yards and Border 
Check Posts. 
Step 
12 
System dispatches confirmation SMS and email to entity holder with new Licence 
Expiry Date, renewal receipt number, and applicable Market Year. Alert schedule 
(BR-AST-94) resets and begins for the new licence period. 
 
  

--- PAGE 179 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 179 of 435 
Annotations — Edge Cases and Ambiguities 
⚠ Edge Cases, Ambiguities & Developer Notes 
EC-01 | Overlapping Market Year Configuration: If the Configuration Manager sets 
conflicting dates across two adjacent Market Years (e.g. Transaction Window End Date of 
Year N extends past the Late Fee Effective Date of Year N+1), the system shall use the dates 
of the Market Year to which the entity's Licence Expiry Date belongs. The system shall 
validate for overlaps at configuration save time and warn the Configuration Manager before 
allowing approval. 
EC-02 | Mid-Year Configuration Change: If the Transaction Window End Date or Late Fee 
Effective Date is changed after transactions have already been accepted in the old 
configuration, the new dates apply only to transactions processed after the effective datetime 
of the configuration change. Prior transactions retain the configuration values that were active 
at the time of processing. No retroactive adjustment of prior receipts is permitted. 
EC-03 | Licence Expiry Mid-Year (Non-31-March): BR-AST-88 specifies that the 
Transaction Window applies to licences expiring on 31 March. If a licence expires on any 
other date (e.g. mid-year suspension or cancellation), the Grace Window does NOT apply — 
the licence is immediately Hard-Blocked on expiry. Clarification required from GAPLMB: 
should a separate "non-standard expiry" grace period be defined? Until confirmed, the system 
applies immediate hard block for non-31-March expiries. 
EC-04 | Renewal Before Expiry Date: A trader may renew before 31 March (pre-emptive 
renewal). In this case: no late fee applies (current date < Late Fee Effective Date). The new 
Licence Expiry Date = 31 March of the next Market Year. The Transaction Window and Late 
Fee rules do not apply to pre-emptive renewals. 
EC-05 | Multiple Premises / Multi-Yard Entities: An entity may hold licences at multiple 
yards. The expiry, transaction window, and late fee rules apply per licence record, not per 
entity. If Yard A's licence is renewed but Yard B's is not, Yard B remains blocked 
independently. 
EC-06 | Pending Renewal at Cutoff Date: If a renewal is submitted before the Renewal 

--- PAGE 180 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 180 of 435 
Cutoff Date but is still pending DA approval on or after the Renewal Cutoff Date, the system 
shall honour the submission date (not the approval date) for cutoff determination. The trader's 
transaction access is maintained in Grace Window status until the renewal is approved or 
rejected. 
EC-07 | AMB-05 RESOLVED — Late Fee Trigger: The late fee trigger is now precisely 
defined as the Late Fee Effective Date configured in M-01 per Market Year. Before this date: 
no late fee. On or after this date: late fee mandatory on all renewals for licences expired in the 
prior Market Year. This resolves the previously open AMB-05 ambiguity (see §5.5.5 
annotations). 
EC-08 | AMB-06 RESOLVED — Late Fee Waiver Workflow: The waiver workflow is 
now fully specified in BR-AST-93. DO raises a waiver request with mandatory justification (≥ 
300 chars); DV forwards to DA; DA approves or rejects with mandatory Rejection Reason 
Code. All outcomes are permanently logged. This resolves the previously open AMB-06 
ambiguity. 
 
  

--- PAGE 181 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 181 of 435

5.7.5 UC-TRD-05: Renewal of Market Functionary Registration (Form BM) — Track A 
Pre-Condition 
Trader has Active or Expiring Track A registration. System alerts 
triggered at 60, 30, 7 days. DO is logged in. No outstanding dues (or 
waiver in place). 
Post-Condition 
Licence Expiry Date extended. Prior year compliance confirmed. 
Renewal history appended to trader record. Trader notified. 
Exception Flow 
Outstanding dues: blocks renewal approval until cleared or DA 
override. Upgrade fee required: system calculates and prompts payment 
via M-05 before renewal finalised.

Alternate Flow 
Applicant declares prior suspension or conviction: DA mandatory

5.7.7 UC-PRE-01: Register New Premises in Premises Master (M-02-PM) 
Use Case ID UC-PRE-01 
Use Case Name Register New Physical Premises in Premises Master 
Module M-02-PM — Premises Master Sub-Module 
Actor(s) DO (initiates), DV (verifies), DA (approves) 
Trigger GAPLMB acquires, constructs, or formally recognises a new 
physical premises unit (shop, stall, godown, office, etc.) that must 
be tracked in the system independently of any occupant. 
Precondition DO is logged in. Location Master and Premises Type Master are 
seeded. DA role is available for approval. 
Main Flow 1. DO navigates to SCR-PRE-01 (Premises Master Registration, 
Directory and Lifecycle). 2. DO selects Yard/Location and 
Premises Type from dropdowns. 3. DO enters Premises Name 
(unique within yard). 4. DO enters Area in sq.m. (mandatory). 5. 
DO optionally enters Length, Width, Height (if one entered, all 
three required). 6. DO uploads supporting document if required. 7. 
DO clicks [Submit for Verification]. Status: Pending Approval. 8. 
DV reviews and clicks [Verify]. 9. DA reviews and clicks 
[Approve]. 10. System auto-generates Premises Number in format 
[YARD-CODE]-[TYPE-CODE]-[NNNN]. 11. Premises Status set 
to Active. Registration Date recorded. 12. Premises now appears in 
Premises Directory and is available for allocation. 
Alternate Flows Duplicate Name: System blocks at step 7 with E-PRE-001. Partial 
Dimensions: System blocks at step 7 with E-PRE-003. DA Rejects: 
Record returns to DO with rejection reason. DO may amend and 

--- PAGE 194 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 194 of 435 
resubmit. 
Postcondition 
(Success) 
A new Premises Master Record exists with Active status and a 
system-generated Premises Number. Record is available for 
Premises Allocation. 
Postcondition (Failure) No Premises Master Record is created. Error message displayed. 
Record remains in draft/rejected state. 
Business Rules BR-PRE-001 through BR-PRE-006 (all in Section 5.2 Functional 
Requirements table). Key rules summary: BR-PRE-001 — 
Premises Number format [YARD-CODE]-[TYPE-CODE]-
[NNNN]; BR-PRE-002 — Premises Name mandatory, unique 
within yard; BR-PRE-003 — Gross Floor Area in sq.m. is 
mandatory; BR-PRE-004 — Dimensions optional but all 3 
required if any one is entered; BR-PRE-005 — Premises Number 
unchanged until Unsafe/Demolished; BR-PRE-006 — Three-tier 
DO→DV→DA workflow required. 
Error Codes E-PRE-001 (duplicate name), E-PRE-002 (invalid area), E-PRE-
003 (partial dimensions), E-PRE-006 (missing unsafe doc). 
Cross-references SCR-PRE-01 (Premises Master Registration, Directory and 
Lifecycle), FR-PRE-001, Section 5.5.0 (Premises Master Record), 
Section 5.5.2 (Premises Allocation Record). 
 
 
5.7.8 UC-NRT-01: Ad-hoc Occupant (Track B) Premises Registration 
Use Case: UC-NRT-01: Ad-hoc Occupant (Track B) Premises Registration 
Trigger: An Ad-hoc Occupant requests to rent one or more GAPLMB premises. 
Pre-Condition: At least one Premises ID exists in the Premises Master (§5.5.0) with Status = 
Active and no current active occupant. 
Actor(s): DO (Yard Officer or HO Officer), DV, DA (Secretary). 

--- PAGE 195 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 195 of 435 
Main Flow: (1) DO searches Premises Directory (SCR-PRE-01) and confirms the Premises ID 
is vacant. (2) DO selects Register Ad-hoc Occupant (Track B) and enters: Entity Name, Contact 
Mobile, Contact Address, PAN (mandatory if annual rent exceeds the TDS threshold per BR-
NRT-04). (3) DO selects the Premises ID(s) to allocate and enters Agreement From Date and 
Monthly Rent. (4) DO uploads the tenancy agreement document (PDF, mandatory). (5) DO 
submits for DV review. (6) DV verifies Entity details, Premises ID vacancy, and document 
completeness. (7) DA reviews and approves. System auto-generates a global Entity ID (format: 
ENT-[YYYY]-[NNNNN]) and creates a Premises Allocation Record (§5.5.2) linking the Entity 
ID to each allocated Premises ID. Sub-type is set to Ad-hoc Occupant; GST flag set per entity 
configuration. 
Post-Condition: Entity ID generated and confirmed. Premises ID status updated to Occupied. 
Tenancy record created under Track B Ad-hoc Occupant sub-type; standard Track B ledger and 
M-03 billing apply. Rent invoicing commences from M-03 on next billing cycle. 
Alternative Flow: If the Ad-hoc Occupant requires additional premises, the DO initiates a new 
Premises Allocation referencing the same Entity ID. No new Entity ID is generated. 
Error Codes: E-NRT-001: Entity Name already has an active Ad-hoc Occupant record at same 
location — confirm duplicate or proceed. E-NRT-002: Premises ID not vacant — cannot 
allocate an occupied or non-active premises. E-NRT-003: Agreement document not uploaded 
— mandatory before submission. E-NRT-004: PAN missing for high-value tenancy (annual rent 
exceeds TDS threshold per BR-NRT-04).

SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 196 of 435

6. M-03: Rent / GST Tax Invoice Online Module 
M-03 MODULE QUICK REFERENCE — Rent / GST Tax Invoice Online Module 
Purpose 
Auto-generate monthly GST tax invoices for all Track A and 
Track B (Non-Govt) entities. Post invoices to the outstanding 
dues ledger and enable online payment. 
User Roles 
System (auto-generation). DA: manual override and write-off 
approval. Trader: self-service payment portal. 
Functional Requirements FR-RENT-001: Monthly GST Invoice Auto-Generation | FR-
RENT-002: GST Rate Configuration | FR-RENT-003: GSTR-1 
Export | FR-RENT-004: Invoice Cancellation and Credit Note | 
FR-RENT-005: TDS on Rent | FR-RENT-006: Outstanding 
Dues and Ageing | FR-RENT-007: Interest on Overdue Rent. 
Full rules: §6.1 
Screens GST Invoice screens: §6.2 — SCR-RENT-01 (Monthly 
Invoice Generation Dashboard) and SCR-RENT-02 (Invoice 
List and Search). 
Data Dictionaries §6.2 GST Tax Invoice Data Dictionary 
Use Cases UC-RENT-01: Monthly GST Invoice Auto-Generation (§6.3) 
Error Codes E-RENT-001 onwards. Full definitions: §6.4 
Integration Points M-02 (Premises Allocation and Premises ID used on invoice) | 
M-05 (Receipts generated on payment) | Tally (nightly export).

7. M-04: Market Fee and Commodities Module 
M-04 MODULE QUICK REFERENCE — Market Fee and Commodities Module 
Purpose 
Record daily commodity arrivals at each yard, calculate Market 
Fee (value-based or quantity-based), manage advance deposits, 
and generate periodic Market Fee returns. 
User Roles 
Trader: self-file returns. DO: counter filing. DV: verifies 
arrivals. DA: approves disputed transactions. Check-post 
Officer: records vehicle arrivals. 
Functional Requirements FR-MKT-001 to FR-MKT-015 (fully sequential). Full rules: 
§7.1 
Screens SCR-MKT-01 to SCR-MKT-08 (§7.8) 
Data Dictionaries §7.2 Market Fee Transaction | §7.3.1 Daily Arrival Record | 
§7.4.1 Commodity Aggregation | §7.5.1 Advance Deposit 
Ledger | §7.7.1 Monthly Returns 
Use Cases UC-MKT-01: Trader Returns Filing (§7.8.1) 
Error Codes E-MKT-001 onwards (§7 error section) 
Integration Points M-02 (trader licence status gates market-fee entry) | M-05 
(advance deposits generate receipts).

BR-MKT-01: Check-post fee = Quantity 
(quintals) × Rate per quintal (from 
configurable rate master per commodity and

configurable per transaction type. BR-MKT-
02: Transaction not finalised without either (a) 
a linked receipt from M-05 for direct payment, 
or (b) confirmation of advance Market Fee 
deposit adjustment (see FR-MKT-007, BR-
MKT-20). BR-MKT-03: Transaction types: 
Local Sale, Import, Export. BR-MKT-04: 
Trader must have valid active licence for the 
commodity. An expired licence blocks all new 
Market Fee transactions for that trader (cross-
ref: BR-AST-06 in M-02). BR-MKT-26: 
Where a trader conducts transactions without a 
valid licence, the system shall allow collection 
of both Market Fee AND a Fine/Penalty as 
separate line items on the same Market Fee 
Receipt (RCP-MF-003). The receipt type in 
this case is identified as “MARKET FEE 
RECEIPT” (e.g. DMR/NNNN/YY-YY format 
for Dodamarg yard). BR-MKT-27: Where a 
Market Fee payment requires refund (e.g.

BR-MKT-48: Purchases from Producers (Qty 
and Value) are auto-populated by summing all

from Traders Value − Total Sales Value. Both 
fields are system-computed and read-only.

Feature Detail 
Recording Basis Arrivals recorded per trader, per commodity, per day at each

Data Sources (a) Arrivals at GAPLMB Border Check Posts; (b) Arrivals

End-of-Day Price Data For each commodity at each yard: Minimum Price (lowest

Monthly Returns Feed Daily arrival data is the primary source for Monthly Returns

Audit Trail All arrival records stored with timestamp, operator ID, yard

7.4 Commodity Arrival Aggregation and Price Determination 
Step Process Description 
Step 1 — Aggregate 
Arrivals 
All trader-wise arrivals for each commodity at each yard are summed 
into a commodity-wise total quantity for the day. 
Step 2 — Compute 
Total Quantity 
Total quantity (quintals, kilograms, or units) = sum of all individual 
trader arrival entries for the commodity on the day at that yard. 
Step 3 — Official 
Daily Prices 
Minimum Price = lowest price recorded. Maximum Price = highest 
price recorded. Modal Price = most frequent (value-weighted if tied). 
These are the official daily market prices for the commodity at the 
yard. 
Publication Official daily prices published on the GAPLMB portal. Used as 
reference data for weekly, fortnightly, and monthly reporting.

7.5 Market Fee Calculation and Ledger Management 
Function Description 
Auto-Calculation System automatically calculates Market Fee payable by each 
trader based on the value of commodities traded, using the 
configurable rate master (per commodity, per location). 
Ledger Posting Calculated Market Fee posted to the trader's ledger (linked to 
Entity ID in M-02) as a receivable amount due to GAPLMB. 
Settlement — Option 1 
(Advance Adjustment) 
Adjustment against advance Market Fee deposits held by 
GAPLMB on behalf of the trader. Advance balance auto-reduced 
on each adjustment. 
Settlement — Option 2 
(Direct Payment) 
Direct payment by the trader via M-05 Receipts to clear 
outstanding Market Fee. 
Advance Deposit Ledger Per-trader ledger of deposits received, adjustments applied, and 
current balance. Alert generated when advance balance falls 
below a configurable minimum threshold.

7.7 Monthly Returns Submission 
Step / Feature Description 
Auto-Population The Monthly Returns Form is automatically populated with all 
arrival data recorded against the trader's Entity ID during the 
month. Data sources: (a) GAPLMB Border Check Post arrivals; 
(b) GAPLMB market yard arrivals. 
T2T Purchases Traders purchasing commodities from other traders within the 
state must separately record T2T transactions. Included in the 
Monthly Return as a distinct category. 
Submission Workflow Trader reviews auto-populated return on the GAPLMB self-
service portal, adds T2T transactions, and submits. Return 
follows DO (Trader) -> DV (Yard Officer) -> DA (Secretary) 
workflow before being marked Final. 
Deadlines and Alerts Submission deadline: configurable (default: 7th of the following 
month). Late submissions trigger automated alerts to Yard DO 
and Head Office. Outstanding returns flagged on Yard Officer 
dashboard. 
Records Retention The finalised Monthly Return is the official statement of a 
trader's market transactions for the month and is permanently 
retained, linked to the trader's Entity ID. 
 
Portal Filing Wizard — Three-Step Flow (FR-MKT-013) 
The GAPLMB portal delivers Returns filing through a guided three-step wizard presented as a 
labelled progress bar. The wizard is accessible via two modes: (a) Trader Self-Filing — the 
trader logs in with Role R-TRD and files their own return; (b) Official Counter Filing — an 
Authorised Official (Role DO or above) selects the trader from the registry and files on their 

--- PAGE 232 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 232 of 435 
behalf. Both modes produce an identical return record; the filing mode is stamped on the 
submission and reproduced on the printed PDF. 
• Step 1 — Select Trader and Period: The user selects the Trader / Commission 
Agent (by name or Licence No.) and the return period (monthly or quarterly). Trader 
details — name, owner, licence number, type, address, and market — are displayed 
for confirmation once a trader is selected. Navigation to Step 2 is blocked until both 
a valid trader and a period are chosen. Quarterly periods are offered in addition to 
monthly; a quarterly return is blocked if any constituent monthly return has already 
been submitted (E-MKT-007). 
• Step 2 — Review Pre-filled Data: The system consolidates all Yard arrival entries 
and Check-post entries for the selected trader and period, grouped by commodity. 
The commodity-wise return table displays Opening Balance (editable), Purchases 
from Producers — Qty and Value (read-only, from Yard records), Purchases from 
Traders / Check-post — Qty and Value (read-only, from Check-post records), Total 
Sales — Qty and Value (trader-entered), and Closing Stock — Qty and Value 
(system-computed). A summary panel shows total value of purchases from 
producers, total value of purchases from traders, and the number of commodities 
with arrivals. Market Fee Payable is computed live and shown at the foot of the 
table. 
• Step 3 — Declare and Submit: A filing summary is presented: trader details, 
period, filing mode, total purchases from producers, total purchases from traders, 
total sales, and Market Fee Payable. The statutory declaration — “I / We hereby 
declare that the information furnished above is true and correct to the best of my / 
our knowledge and belief” — is displayed above the Submit button. On successful 
submission the system generates the Acknowledgement Reference Number (format: 
GAPLMB/[MARKET_CODE]/[YYYY]/[MM]/[ASSET_ID]/[NNNNN]) and offers 
an immediate option to print or download the PDF return (FR-MKT-015, BR-MKT-
53 to BR-MKT-56). 
Quarterly Returns 
Traders may opt to file a Quarterly Return in lieu of three individual Monthly Returns where 
this is permitted under the applicable Act. The period selector in Step 1 offers both monthly and 
quarterly options (Q1: Jan–Mar, Q2: Apr–Jun, Q3: Jul–Sep, Q4: Oct–Dec). A quarterly return 

--- PAGE 233 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 233 of 435 
consolidates all Yard and Check-post arrival data across the three constituent months. The 
system blocks a quarterly return if any individual monthly return for a constituent month 
already exists in SUBMITTED, VERIFIED, or APPROVED status for the same trader (E-
MKT-007). The deadline for quarterly returns is the 7th of the month following the quarter end 
(configurable per BR-MKT-69).

7.8 Screen Descriptions — M-04 Module 
SCR-MKT-01 — Market Fee Collection Entry 
Purpose Record a Market Fee transaction for commodity arrivals at a yard gate 
or border check post. 
Actor(s) DO (Gate Clerk / Yard Officer) 
Key Input Fields Entity ID / Licence No. (search), Commodity (from master), Quantity + 
Unit, Transaction Price (market yard), Vehicle Reg. No. 
(Import/Export), Transaction Type (Local Sale / Import / Export), 
Payment Mode. 
Primary Actions [Calculate Fee] (auto), [Collect Payment → M-05], [Adjust Advance 
Deposit], [Print Receipt] 
Special Notes Fee auto-calculated based on transaction type: check-post = Qty × Rate; 
market yard = Value × %. Expired trader licence blocks entry (E-AST-
002). Advance deposit balance shown in sidebar with low-balance alert. 
 
SCR-MKT-02 — Daily Arrival Register 
Purpose View and manage trader-wise daily commodity arrival records for a 
selected yard and date. 
Actor(s) DO (Yard Officer), DV, DA, Auditor 
Key Input Fields Yard / Location, Date, Commodity filter, Trader filter, Status filter 
(Draft / Submitted / Verified / Approved). 
Primary Actions [Add Arrival Record], [View / Edit (Draft only)], [Submit for 
Verification], [Run End-of-Day Aggregation], [Export Arrivals 
Register] 
Special Notes End-of-day aggregation computes official Min/Max/Modal prices per 
commodity and publishes to GAPLMB portal. Price columns remain 
blank until aggregation run. 

--- PAGE 237 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 237 of 435 
 
SCR-MKT-03 — Monthly Returns Dashboard 
Purpose Trader-facing portal screen to review auto-populated monthly return, 
add T2T purchases, and submit. 
Actor(s) Trader (R-TRD via portal), DO / Yard Officer (on behalf of trader at 
counter), DV (verification), DA (final approval) 
Key Input Fields Return Month / Year (auto-set), Total Arrivals Qty and Value (read-
only, auto-populated), T2T Purchase Qty and Value (trader-entered), 
Remarks. 
Primary Actions [Load Pre-filled Data] (Step 1→2), [Edit Opening Balance], [Enter 
Sales Qty and Value], [Back to Edit Data] (Step 3→2), [Declare and 
Submit] (Step 3), [Download / Print PDF] (post-submission), [File 
Another Return] (resets wizard), [View Past Returns] 
Special Notes Step 1: Trader/period selection with inline trader detail card and filing-
mode toggle (Self-Filing / Official). Step 2: Commodity table with 
colour-coded column groups — green for Yard (Purchases from 
Producers), blue for Check-post (Purchases from Traders), amber for 
Sales (trader-entered), gray for Closing Stock (computed). Opening 
Balance is pre-populated from prior return’s Closing Stock; editable. A 
summary metric panel shows totals for purchases from producers, 
purchases from traders, and commodity count. Market Fee Payable (₹1 
per ₹100 of produce purchased from producers) is computed live and 
shown at the table foot. Step 3 (Declaration): shows filing summary, 
statutory declaration, and Submit button. Post-submission: 
acknowledgement reference number displayed; PDF download offered 
immediately. Deadline reminder banner shown from the 1st to 7th of 
the following month. Overdue returns highlighted in red. Late 
submission flag auto-set if submitted after deadline. For quarterly 
returns, the period selector shows Q1–Q4 options; quarterly filing 

--- PAGE 238 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 238 of 435 
blocked if any constituent monthly return already exists (E-MKT-007). 
 
SCR-MKT-04 — Returns History and PDF Download 
Purpose View all past filed returns for a trader, check workflow status, and 
download PDF of any previously filed return. 
Actor(s) Trader (R-TRD via portal), DO / Yard Officer, DV, DA, Auditor 
Key Input Fields Entity ID / Licence No. (auto-set for self-filing; selectable for officials), 
Period filter, Status filter (All / Draft / Submitted / Verified / Approved 
/ Rejected). 
Primary Actions [View Return Detail], [Download PDF] (any status), [File New Return] 
(navigates to SCR-MKT-03), [Request Recall] (Approved returns — 
DA only, triggers E-MKT-006 flow) 
Special Notes Returns are listed in reverse chronological order. Overdue periods (no 
return filed and deadline passed) are shown in red. Late-filed returns are 
flagged with a “Late” badge. PDF download is available for all return 
statuses. Traders (R-TRD) can only view their own returns; Officials 
can view returns for any trader within their jurisdiction. 
7.8.1 UC-MKT-01: Trader Returns Filing — Self-Service and Official Counter 
Use Case Field Detail 
Use Case ID and 
Name 
UC-MKT-01: Trader Returns Filing — Self-Service and Official 
Counter 
Actor(s) Primary: Trader / Commission Agent (Role R-TRD) or Authorised 
Official (Role DO). Secondary: DV (Yard Officer — verification), DA 
(Secretary — final approval). 
Pre-conditions (1) Trader holds a valid, active licence in M-02. (2) At least one Daily 
Arrival Record (Yard or Check-post) exists for the trader and period, 
OR the trader has stock from a prior period (Opening Balance > 0). (3) 

--- PAGE 239 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 239 of 435 
No approved return already exists for the same trader and period (else 
E-MKT-006). (4) Actor is authenticated and holds Role R-TRD (self-
filing) or Role DO or above (official filing). 
Normal Flow 1. Actor navigates to SCR-MKT-03 and selects filing mode (Self / 
Official). 2. Actor selects Entity ID / Licence No. and return period; 
system displays trader detail card for confirmation. 3. Actor clicks 
[Load Pre-filled Data]; system retrieves and consolidates Yard and 
Check-post arrival records for the period, grouped by commodity, and 
presents the commodity-wise table (Step 2). 4. Actor reviews auto-
populated columns (read-only) and enters or adjusts Opening Balance 
and Total Sales Qty / Value for each commodity. 5. System computes 
Closing Stock and Market Fee Payable in real time. 6. Actor clicks 
[Review and Declare]; system presents Step 3 filing summary including 
total figures and the statutory declaration text. 7. Actor reads the 
declaration and clicks [Submit Return]; system validates all entries, 
generates Acknowledgement Reference Number (BR-MKT-53), creates 
the Monthly Returns Record (status: SUBMITTED), and presents the 
success screen with the reference number and [Download PDF] option. 
8. Return enters DO → DV → DA workflow for verification and 
approval (BR-MKT-70). 
Alternate Flows AF-01 (Quarterly Filing): At Step 1 actor selects a quarterly period. 
System checks no constituent monthly return exists (else E-MKT-007). 
System aggregates three months of Yard and Check-post data; flow 
continues from Step 2. AF-02 (No Arrivals in Period): System presents 
the commodity table with all Qty/Value columns at zero; trader may 
still enter Opening Balance and Sales or submit a nil return. AF-03 
(Back Navigation): Actor clicks [Back to Edit Data] on Step 3; system 
returns to Step 2 with all previously entered values preserved. AF-04 
(Late Filing): Actor submits after the deadline; system sets Late 
Submission flag TRUE (BR-MKT-69), stamps submission timestamp, 

--- PAGE 240 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 240 of 435 
and alerts Yard DO and HO; filing proceeds normally. 
Exceptions E-MKT-006: Return already submitted for period — block at Step 1. E-
MKT-007: Quarterly return blocked because constituent monthly return 
already filed — block at Step 1. E-MKT-008: Future period selected — 
block at Step 1. E-MKT-009: Declared Sales Qty exceeds available 
stock — block at Step 2 before actor can proceed to Step 3. 
Post-conditions A Monthly Returns Record is created with status SUBMITTED, linked 
to the trader’s Entity ID. Acknowledgement Reference Number is 
generated and immutably stored. Market Fee Payable is recorded 
against the return and posted to the trader’s M-02 Entity ID ledger as a 
pending debit. PDF is generated and attached to the record. Return is 
placed in the DV / DA approval queue. Late Submission flag is set if 
applicable.

gateway. 
Actor(s) Trader (External)

5) 
Primary Actions [Select Invoices], [Proceed to Pay] → Payment Gateway 
Special Notes Payment gateway redirect: SBI ePay / NSDL / RazorpayGov (per 
GAPLMB decision). Gateway selection required: §18, Item 12. On 
success: redirect back with receipt PDF download. 
 
SCR-RCP-02 — Counter Receipt Generation (Offline) 
Purpose Counter screen for DO to record cash/cheque/DD/NEFT payments 
received in person. 
Actor(s) DO (Yard Officer, Accounts Section) 
Key Input Fields Payer Name (auto-fill from Trader/Employee or manual for Misc.). 
Revenue Head. Linked Invoice/Demand No. Amount (≤ outstanding 
balance). Mode of Payment. Transaction Ref. No. (for non-cash). Date 
of Payment. 
Primary Actions [Look Up Outstanding] (by Trader ID / Entity ID), [Generate Receipt], 
[Print Receipt], [Send Receipt by Email/SMS] 
Special Notes Cash amount > ₹10,000: warning shown (IT Act threshold). Receipt 
No. is generated on server at moment of successful payment 
confirmation. Two copies printed.

SCR-RCP-03 — Receipt Search and Verification 
Purpose: Search, view, and verify any issued receipt by Receipt No., Entity ID / Licence No., 
entity name, date range, or revenue head. Supports counter-verification requests and duplicate 
print. 
Actor(s): DV (Accounts Officer), DA (Secretary), Auditor, Trader (own receipts only via 
portal) 
Key Input Fields: Search bar: Receipt No. / Entity ID / Licence No. / Payer Name. Filters: 
Revenue Head, Date Range, Location, Payment Mode, Status (Issued / Cancelled). 
Primary Actions: [Search], [View Receipt Details], [Download PDF Receipt], [Send by 
Email/SMS], [Cancel Receipt] (DA only — with Credit Note), [Export to Excel] 
Special Notes: Receipts cancelled after DA approval generate an auto Credit Note and reverse 
the ledger entry. QR code on receipt is verifiable at https://gaplmb.goa.gov.in/verify. 
SCR-RCP-04 — Daily Reconciliation Dashboard 
Purpose End-of-day reconciliation view for Accounts Officer. 
Actor(s) DV (Accounts Officer), DA (Secretary) 
Key Input Fields Date selector. Location. Revenue Head. Columns: Opening 
Outstanding, Receipts Today (count + amount), Mode-wise breakdown, 
Closing Outstanding. 
Special Notes Discrepancy alert sent to Accounts Officer email at 18:00 hrs if 
unresolved. 
 
8.3 Tally Ledger Mapping and Export 
GAPLMB maintains its accounts in Tally. Every receipt generated by the IOMS must map each 
line item to its corresponding Tally ledger head so that data can be exported and posted without 
manual re-entry. The system shall achieve this through a configurable Tally Ledger Master and 
dynamic, ledger-driven receipt forms. The three Tally receipt types defined in the GAPLMB 
Tally configuration are: (a) Market Fee Receipt, (b) Rent Receipt, and (c) Yard Receipt. All 38 
ledger heads drawn from the GAPLMB Tally ledger file (“Tally_ledgers.xlsx”) are pre-seeded 
in the system at go-live and managed through the M-01 Configuration Console. 

--- PAGE 253 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 253 of 435

SCR-RCP-05 — Undeposited Receipts and Deposit Entry 
 
Purpose 
Display all undeposited cash and cheque receipts for the user’s 
location, and allow the Depositor to record a bank deposit against 
selected receipts. 
Actor(s) DO / Accounts Officer (Depositor role) 
Key Input Fields 
Location (auto from user profile). Date Range filter. Undeposited 
receipts grid: Receipt No. │ Date │ Payer Name │ Payment Mode 
(Cash/Cheque) │ Amount │ Days Since Issue │ Select checkbox. 
Bank Account dropdown (filtered per FR-RCP-010 — location and 
user). Deposit Date (defaults to today; may be today or next working 
day). Summary panel: Selected Count, Total Cash Selected (₹), Total 
Cheque Selected (₹), Grand Total (₹). 
Primary Actions 
[Select All Cash] [Select All Cheque] [Deselect All] [Submit Deposit] 
[Defer Selected to Next Day] [Export Undeposited List] 
Special Notes 
Each receipt must be deposited in full — amount column is read-only 
(BR-RCP-36). Only one bank account may be selected per deposit 
batch (BR-RCP-37). Multi-account deposit is blocked. Receipts with 
Mode of Payment = Online or QR Code are not shown in this list 
(BR-RCP-34). On [Submit Deposit], the system generates a Deposit 
Ref. No. and changes receipt status to Deposited (Pending 
Verification). The DO may print or email the Deposit Summary slip.

--- PAGE 266 ---

Undeposited Receipt (Date). Detail grid: Receipt No. │ Date │ Payer

RCP-005 (BR-RCP-56). End-of-day Cash-in-Hand Summary is auto-
emailed at 18:00 hrs to Accounts Officer and DA (BR-RCP-55). The 
consolidated view (DV/DA) shows a location-wise summary row with 
a drill-down to individual receipt details.

8.6 Document Print Mode Selection 
This section defines the cross-cutting print mode selection capability that applies to all printable 
documents generated by the IOMS — including GST Tax Invoices, receipts, Pre-Receipts, 
notices, certificates, and outward correspondence. All printing is initiated from within the 
respective module screens; this section governs the print-mode choice that is presented at the 
point of printing. 
 
FR-PRT-001 Document Print Mode Selection 
Description The system shall support two print modes for all printable documents: 
(1) Plain Paper (System Template) — the full document including 
GAPLMB header, logo, address, and statutory content is rendered and 
printed by the system on standard A4 paper; and (2) Pre-Printed 
Stationery — only the transactional body content is printed, with all 
header elements suppressed, sized and aligned for placement on pre-
printed official letterhead stationery loaded by the user. At the point of 
printing, the user shall select the applicable print mode from a print-

--- PAGE 269 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 269 of 435 
mode selector presented on screen. The system shall not auto-detect or 
validate the stationery type loaded in the printer. 
Business Rules BR-PRT-01 (Supported Print Modes): The system shall support exactly 
two print modes for all printable documents across all modules: (a) 
Plain Paper (System Template) and (b) Pre-Printed Stationery. No other 
print modes are required. BR-PRT-02 (Plain Paper Mode — Full 
Render): When the user selects “Plain Paper (System Template)”, the 
system shall render and print the complete document including: 
GAPLMB official header (organisation name, address, contact details), 
logo placeholder, document title, all transactional content, QR code, and 
statutory footer. BR-PRT-03 (Pre-Printed Stationery Mode — Header 
Suppression): When the user selects “Pre-Printed Stationery”, the 
system shall suppress all header elements (logo, organisation name, 
address block) and print only the transactional content body, sized and 
aligned for the standard pre-printed stationery format. Alignment 
parameters shall be configurable by the System Administrator without 
code change. BR-PRT-04 (Letterhead Responsibility): The official 
letterhead design, logo, format, statutory content, and branding are the 
sole responsibility of the client organisation (GAPLMB). The system 
shall not generate, supply, or validate official letterhead formats. BR-
PRT-05 (Stationery Loading Responsibility): When “Pre-Printed 
Stationery” is selected, it is the user’s responsibility to load the correct 
pre-printed stationery in the printer before initiating printing. The 
system shall not detect, validate, or confirm stationery type. BR-PRT-06 
(Compliance Responsibility): Legal, statutory, and branding correctness 
of printed documents produced on pre-printed stationery remains the 
responsibility of the client organisation. The system ensures only data 
accuracy and configurable formatting support. BR-PRT-07 (Scope): 
FR-PRT-001 applies to all printable outputs across all modules 
including but not limited to: GST Tax Invoices (M-03), Market Fee 
Receipts (M-04/M-05), Rent Receipts (M-05), Pre-Receipts (M-02/M-

--- PAGE 270 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 270 of 435 
03), Payment Vouchers (M-06), Trader Registration Certificates (M-
02), Leave Encashment Certificates (M-01), Correspondence and 
Notices (M-09), and any other document for which a [Print] action is 
provided. 
Screen Behaviour When any [Print] action is initiated, a Print Mode Selector dialog shall 
be presented to the user with two radio button options: ◉ Plain Paper 
(System Template) and ○ Pre-Printed Stationery. The system shall 
remember the user’s last selected print mode as a default for the current 
session (session-level preference; not persisted across logins). A print 
preview shall be available for both modes before the final print 
command is issued. The print preview shall reflect the selected mode 
(full header visible for Plain Paper; header suppressed for Pre-Printed 
Stationery). On [Print]: the system-generated PDF is sent to the selected 
printer or downloaded for manual printing as configured by the user’s 
workstation settings. 
Priority High 
 
  

--- PAGE 271 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 271 of 435

Fields 
Work Ref. No. (auto-filled), Contractor Name (auto-filled), Bill No., Bill

SCR-CNST-03 — AMC Register 
Purpose 
Register and manage Annual Maintenance Contracts per yard/location with 
contractor, period, bill schedule, and linked payment vouchers. 
Actor(s) DO (Yard/HO Officer), DV (Accounts Officer), DA (Secretary), Auditor 
Key Input 
Fields 
AMC Ref. No. (system-generated per BR-AMC-01), Location, Contractor,

Document upload (PDF). 
Primary 
Actions 
[Register New AMC], [View AMC], [Renew AMC], [Link Bill Voucher from 
M-06], [Generate AMC Invoice] (manual trigger — no automatic generation; 
all billing cycles are manual per BR-AMC-04), [Export AMC List] 
Special Notes 
AMC expiry triggers alerts at 60 and 30 days (POP + SMS per BR-AMC-02). 
Renewal must start on or before previous AMC end date - no gap (BR-AMC-
03, E-AMC-001 blocks renewal with gap).

13. M-10: User Account and Role-Based Access Control 
M-10 MODULE QUICK REFERENCE — User Account and Role-Based Access Control 
Purpose 
Create and manage user accounts for all GAPLMB staff. 
Assign roles (DO, DV, DA, Auditor, Config Manager). Every 
M-01 employee record is coupled to exactly one user account. 
User Roles 
System Administrator: creates and manages all user accounts. 
DA: approves role changes. 
Functional Requirements FR-USR-001 to FR-USR-005 (sequential). Full rules: §13.1 
Screens SCR-USR-01 to SCR-USR-03 (§13) 
Data Dictionaries §13 User and RBAC data dictionary | §13.2 Role Permission 
Matrix 

--- PAGE 298 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 298 of 435 
Use Cases UC-USR-01 (§13) 
Error Codes E-USR-001 onwards (§13.3) 
Integration Points M-01 (every employee has one user account) | All modules 
(RBAC governs access to every screen). 
 
CRITICAL MODULE: All access to the IOMS is governed by this module. No User ID can exist 
without a corresponding Active Employee record in M-01. This coupling is enforced at the 
database level by a referential integrity constraint and at the application level. 
13.1 Functional Requirements 
FR 
ID 
Feature Description Business Rules Priority 
FR-

001 
Employee-

when Employee Status = 
Active in M-01. System

User IDs.

creating a User ID, system

active in M-01 (real-time 
API call). BR-USR-02:

exactly one User ID (1:1). 
BR-USR-03: User ID

[EMPLOYEE-ID]; 
immutable. 
Critical 
FR-
