14.2 Security Requirements 
NFR ID Requirement 
NFR-SEC-
01 
All communications shall be enforced over HTTPS (TLS 1.3 preferred; TLS 
1.2 minimum). HTTP shall be strictly disabled at the web-server and load-
balancer level. 
NFR-SEC-
02 
The system shall support NIC/GoG SSO as the primary authentication 
mechanism, with a local username/password fallback subject to complexity 
rules in BR-USR-10. 
NFR-SEC-
03 
Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA) shall be enforced for: Data Approver (DA 
/ Secretary), System Administrator, and Accounts Officer. 
NFR-SEC-
04 
Aadhaar: Authentication via Aadhaar is not implemented in this version. All 
Aadhaar data stored exclusively in masked format (XXXX-XXXX-1234). No 
raw value shall be persisted, logged, or transmitted. 
NFR-SEC-
05 
The system shall maintain an immutable audit trail for all data operations. No 
audit record shall be modified or deleted by any user or process. 

--- PAGE 307 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 307 of 435 
NFR-SEC-
06 
The system shall comply with the OWASP Top 10. Mandatory OWASP-based 
security testing shall be completed and documented before go-live. 
NFR-SEC-
07 
All data at rest shall be encrypted using AES-256. All database backups shall 
be encrypted using the same standard. 
NFR-SEC-
08 
The system shall enforce an automatic session timeout of 30 minutes of 
inactivity. Timeout duration shall be configurable by the System 
Administrator. 
NFR-SEC-
09 
Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) shall be enforced at both the UI layer and 
the API layer. No API endpoint shall be accessible without valid 
authentication and authorised role. 
NFR-SEC-
10 
All database interactions shall use parameterised queries or ORM-generated 
queries exclusively. Dynamic SQL string concatenation with user input is 
strictly prohibited. Code review shall include automated static analysis (SAST) 
to detect injection vulnerabilities before each release. 
NFR-SEC-
11 
All user-supplied input rendered in HTML context shall be escaped using a 
context-aware output encoding library (e.g., OWASP Java Encoder or 
equivalent). A Content-Security-Policy (CSP) header shall be enforced at the 
web server level. 
NFR-SEC-
12 
CSRF tokens shall be generated per session and validated on all state-changing 
HTTP requests (POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH). The SameSite=Strict cookie 
attribute shall be applied to all session cookies. 
NFR-SEC-
13 
A penetration test by a CERT-IN empanelled third-party shall be conducted 
before go-live and annually thereafter. Critical and High findings must be 
remediated within 30 days of report delivery. Pen-test scope covers all 10 
modules, all user roles, and all external interfaces. 
14.3 Availability and Reliability 
NFR ID Metric Requirement 

--- PAGE 308 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 308 of 435 
NFR-AVAIL-01 Uptime The system shall maintain 
99.5% uptime per calendar 
month, excluding planned 
maintenance windows. 
NFR-AVAIL-02 Planned Maintenance Planned maintenance shall be 
scheduled between 23:00 and 
05:00 IST. Advance notice of 
at least 24 hours shall be 
provided to all users. 
NFR-AVAIL-03 RTO The system shall achieve a 
Recovery Time Objective 
(RTO) of ≤ 4 hours for 
critical modules (M-04 
Market Fee, M-05 Receipts). 
NFR-AVAIL-04 RPO The system shall achieve a 
Recovery Point Objective 
(RPO) of ≤ 1 hour, enforced 
via daily automated database 
backups and hourly 
transaction log backups. 
NFR-AVAIL-05 Disaster Recovery A Disaster Recovery (DR) 
site shall be maintained at a 
secondary NIC/SDC location. 
Failover capability shall be 
tested biannually and results 
documented. 
NFR-AVAIL-06 Offline Graceful Handling The system shall provide 
graceful degradation for 
check-post users during 

--- PAGE 309 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 309 of 435 
connectivity loss, with local 
queuing of data entries and 
automatic synchronisation on 
reconnect. 
 
14.4 Usability and Accessibility — Mobile Readiness 
NFR ID Requirement 
NFR-USA-01 The system shall comply with GIGW v3 (Guidelines for Indian Government 
Websites). 
NFR-USA-02 The system shall implement responsive design, ensuring all screens are fully 
functional on viewport widths from 320 px (mobile) to 1920 px (desktop). 
Architected as a Mobile-First Progressive Web App (PWA). 
NFR-USA-03 The system shall be compatible with major screen readers (NVDA, JAWS) to 
meet WCAG 2.2 Level AA accessibility standards. 
NFR-USA-04 The system shall support Indian language display (Konkani / Marathi) using 
Unicode/UTF-8 encoding. Language labels shall be configurable by the 
System Administrator. 
NFR-USA-05 The system shall use a minimum font size of 14 px for body text and 16 px 
for input field labels. 
NFR-USA-06 The system shall be installable as a PWA on Android 11+ and iOS 16+ home 
screens and shall support offline read operations for Border Check Post users. 
NFR-USA-07 The REST/JSON API layer shall be designed to support consumption by 
native mobile clients (React Native / Flutter) without requiring API changes 
(see §15.1). 
14.5 Maintainability and Scalability 
NFR ID Requirement 

--- PAGE 310 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 310 of 435 
NFR-MNT-
01 
The system shall implement a three-tier architecture (Presentation, Business 
Logic, Data) with clean separation of concerns between layers. 
NFR-MNT-
02 
All system-wide configurable parameters (pay rates, TA/DA rates, leave 
rules, GST rates, fee rates) shall be manageable through the M-01 
Configuration Console without requiring code deployment. 
NFR-MNT-
03 
The data access layer shall use a database-agnostic ORM to enable future 
database migration with minimal code impact. 
NFR-MNT-
04 
The application tier shall support horizontal scaling via a load balancer to 
accommodate growth in user load beyond the baseline 200-user specification. 
NFR-MNT-
05 
The system shall implement REST API versioning (v1, v2...) to support 
future native mobile clients and third-party integrations without breaking 
existing integrations (see §15.1). 
NFR-MNT-
06 
The development team shall achieve a minimum of 80% automated unit test 
coverage for all Critical-priority functional requirements across all modules. 
15. System Architecture and Interfaces 
 
NOTE — Design Deliverable Required: A System Context Diagram and a Cross-Module 
Integration Map must be produced as separate design artefacts during the High-Level 
Design (HLD) phase and attached to this section before design freeze. The Context 
Diagram shall show GAPLMB IOMS as the central boundary with all external actors and 
data flows. The Integration Map shall show the 10 modules (M-01 to M-10) as nodes with 
directed dependency edges (e.g., M-01→M-10 Employee-User coupling; M-02→M-03 
Premises→Invoice; M-04→M-05 Market Fee→Receipt).

17. Constraints and Assumptions 
17.1 Constraints 
Constraint Description 
Infrastructure The system shall be hosted on a Government-approved Public Cloud 
platform (currently AWS). Migration to an alternate Government-
approved platform shall not require application changes. 
Aadhaar Data 
Protection 
Raw or unmasked Aadhaar data must never be stored, displayed, 
processed, or transmitted at any stage, in any component of the 
system. 
GST Compliance All GST invoice generation, return data (GSTR-1, GSTR-3B), and 
TDS calculations shall conform to GSTN specifications and current 
Indian tax law. 
Source Code Must be maintained in a Government-approved version control 
repository (NIC GitLab or equivalent). 
Integration Standards All external API integrations (GSTN, Payment Gateway, NIC/GoG 
SSO) shall be implemented in accordance with the terms and 
technical specifications published by the respective Government or 
approved service providers. 
17.2 Assumptions 
Assumption 
ID 
Description 
ASM-01 Aadhaar numbers are collected solely as a reference identifier and stored in 
masked format (XXXX-XXXX-1234) only. No UIDAI eKYC integration is 
required in Phase 1. 
ASM-02 GAPLMB will ensure a minimum 4 Mbps internet connectivity at all 

--- PAGE 318 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 318 of 435 
locations (HO, Sub-Yards, Check Posts) before system go-live. 
ASM-03 Government of Goa standard service and leave rules (as specified in the 
referenced GoG Service Rules) apply to all GAPLMB employees. 
ASM-04 The applicable GST rate for commercial rent services is CGST 9% + SGST 
9% (total 18%). This rate is configurable and may be updated by the System 
Administrator without code change. 
ASM-05 TDS on rent under Section 194-I of the Income Tax Act 1961 is applicable 
when annual rent per tenant exceeds Rs. 2,40,000. Both threshold and TDS 
rate are configurable. 
ASM-06 The payment gateway (SBI ePay, NSDL, or RazorpayGov) shall be formally 
selected and approved by GAPLMB before M-05 (Receipts) development 
begins (§18, Item 12). 
ASM-07 GAPLMB shall provide a complete and validated commodity master list 
(commodity codes, names, and default Market Fee rates) to the development 
team before M-04 build commences. 
ASM-08 The GAPLMB IT team or a designated system integrator shall manage server 
provisioning, domain configuration, and SSL certificate management before 
go-live. 
ASM-09 GoG service rules governing employee leave, pay levels, and retirement age 
shall remain unchanged during Phase 1 development. Any legislative change 
shall be treated as a formal Change Request. 
ASM-10 All external APIs (GSTN, NIC/GoG SSO, SMS Gateway, Payment Gateway) 
will be available with stable specifications during the system build phase. 
Post-integration API changes shall be managed as Change Requests. 
ASM-11 GAPLMB shall conduct UAT with nominated representatives from all user 
classes within 30 days of each module being made available in the UAT 
environment. 

--- PAGE 319 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 319 of 435 
ASM-12 Browser-based access is assumed for all internal users. The system is not 
required to support Internet Explorer or browsers more than two major 
versions old. 
ASM-13 The Biometric Attendance System (BAS) at all locations shall use an 
integration SDK compatible with the REST/JSON API specified in §15.2 (I-
EXT-07) before the attendance integration feature is activated. 
17.3 Dependencies 
Dependency Description 
M-01 (HRMS) — 
Prerequisite for All 
Modules 
M-01 is a prerequisite for all other modules. No User ID (M-10), 
TA/DA bill (M-06), or leave record can be created until the 
Employee Master is operational. 
M-02 (Trader) — 
Prerequisite for M-03, M-
04, M-05 
M-02 must be operational before M-03, M-04, or M-05 can 
function. All financial transactions reference an Entity ID from 
M-02 (with Licence No. as the user-facing reference for Track A 
entities). 
M-05 (Receipts) — 
Depends on M-03 and M-
04 
M-05 depends on M-03 (for GST Invoice receipts) and M-04 (for 
Market Fee receipts). Receipt numbers in M-05 are linked back 
to the originating invoice or transaction. 
M-10 (RBAC) — 
Depends on M-01 
User account provisioning requires a valid, Active Employee 
record in M-01 and cannot proceed independently. 
GSTN API (I-EXT-02) The GSTN API integration must be configured and tested before 
M-03 GST invoice posting functionality goes live. 
Payment Gateway (I-
EXT-03) 
The Payment Gateway must be formally selected by GAPLMB 
and integrated before online payment features in M-05 are 
activated (§18, Item 12).

19.3 Appendix C — Requirements Traceability Matrix (RTM) 
Requirement IDs in this document are the definitive, final identifiers for all functional 
requirements. 
The following table maps critical functional requirements to their associated test cases. Status = 
Open indicates the test case is yet to be created/executed pending development commencement. 
All test cases listed here form the minimum UAT (User Acceptance Testing) scope; no FR with 
Priority = Critical may be signed off with Status = Open at UAT entry. The development team 
must produce a Test Case Specification (TCS) document for each TC-ID below, covering: (a) 
pre-conditions, (b) test steps, (c) expected result, (d) pass/fail criteria. The RTM must be 
updated to “Pass” for all Critical items before GAPLMB issues a UAT sign-off. Items marked 
High or Medium may be deferred to Regression testing at GAPLMB’s discretion with DA 
written approval. Acceptance criteria for each module are governed by the Business Rules (BR-
*) defined in Sections 4–13 of this SRS — test cases must validate each BR explicitly.

19.4 Appendix D — Form Layouts 
This appendix presents the standardised UI form layouts for each major data entry screen across 
all 10 IOMS modules. Each layout shows the field label, input widget type, and mandatory / 
optional status. All forms follow the three-tier workflow (DO → DV → DA) unless explicitly 
noted as single-step. All requirements in this document are binding and ready for design and 
development. 
D.1 Employee Registration / Edit Form (SCR-EMP-02, M-01 HRMS)

19.6 Appendix F — Receipt and Certificate Layouts 
This appendix presents the standardised layouts for all receipts and certificates generated by the 
IOMS. All documents include a QR code that can be verified at 
https://gaplmb.goa.gov.in/verify. PDF versions carry the digital signature of the issuing officer 
and the GAPLMB official seal. The layouts below show the prescribed field order; formatting 
(logos, letterhead) will be applied during UI development.

System Field Notes for RCP-MF-003: 
Receipt No. format: [YardPrefix]/[YY-YY]/[NNNNN] — e.g. PF/25-26/00142, where PF is the 
yard-specific prefix configured in the system for that yard (the prefix is assigned by the System 
Administrator per yard via the M -01 Configuration Console before go -live; yard prefix codes 
are listed in Appendix A), 25 -26 is the financial year, and 00142 is the 5 -digit zero -padded 
sequential number, resetting to 00001 on 1 April each year per yard. The system generates this 
automatically on payment confirmation (BR -AST-62, BR -MKT-25, BR -AST-73). Payment 
modes accepted: Cash, Cheque (provisional until bank confirmation), QR Code, Net Banking. 
Receipt is available as PDF download and can be reprinted from any authorised login (BR -
AST-62). Identical layout for both Original (trader copy) and Counterfoil (GAPLMB copy). 
GSTIN/UIN: 30AAALT1317M1Z6.

TERMS AND CONDITIONS 
(1) The Registration holder shall abide by the provisions of the said Act and the Rules and the 
conditions of Agreement entered into by the Registration holder with the State Marketing 
Officer/Secretary of Marketing Board.  
(2) The Registration is not transferable.  
(3) This Registration may be suspended or cancelled in accordance with the provisions of the 
said Act and the Rules made thereunder.  
(4) In the event of suspension or cancellation, it shall be surrendered to the State Marketing 
Officer/Secretary of Marketing Board. 
(5) The Registration holder shall carry on business as a Trader only at such places for which 
the Registration is issued.  
(6) The Registration holder shall pay market fees and supervision charges prescribed to 
GAPLMB.  
(7) The Registration holder should not adulterate or cause any declared agricultural produce to 
be adulterated.  
(8) The Registration holder shall help the State Marketing Officer/Secretary in preventing 
evasion of market fees.  
(9) The Registration holder after grant of Registration shall within 15 days inform about the 
authorised representative.  
(10) The Registration holder shall maintain books, registers and records in the manner 
required by the State Marketing Officer/Secretary and make them available for inspection. 
(11) The Registration holder shall furnish information and returns to the State Marketing 
Officer/Secretary as required from time to time.  
(12) The Registration holder shall settle the prices of agricultural produce according to the 
manner provided under the bye-laws.  
(13) The Registration holder shall, if the declared agricultural produce is sold through his 
agency or by him, pay to the seller the price of the agricultural produce on the same day.  
(14) The Registration holder shall not solicit or receive any fees or recover charges other than 
those he is entitled to receive or recover under the Act and Bye-laws.  
(15) The Registration holder shall not make or recover any trade allowance.  
(16) The Registration holder shall provide for authorised weights and measures.  

--- PAGE 373 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 373 of 435 
(17) The Registration holder shall pay to the registered weighman or measures and hamal only 
at the rates approved by the State Marketing Officer/Secretary and shall not employ them for 
household or private work.  
(18) The Registration holder shall inform the State Marketing Officer/Secretary of any change 
in constitution.  
(19) The Registration holder shall refer all disputes in relation to the marketing of declared 
notified Agricultural Produce in the manner prescribed in Act, Rule and Bye-laws. 
Renewal of Registration

System Field Notes for CERT-LIC-001: 
Licence No. is a system-generated sequential integer (e.g. 10231, 10232, 10238) assigned by the 
Secretary at the time of approval — unique system-wide across all yards and market years. 
Licence fee receipt format: [YardCode]/[YY-YY]/[NNNNN] (e.g. MSA/25-26/04367). Security 
Deposit receipt uses same format. Validity always ends on 31-03-[YYYY] (end of market year) 
regardless of date of issue. Renewal receipt type: Yard Receipt, containing Licence Renewal 
Fee ([Configurable]), Sale of Application Form ([Configurable]), Godown Registration Fee 
([Configurable]). New licence receipt contains: Licence Fee ([Configurable]), Godown 
Registration Fee ([Configurable]), Supply of Stationery ([Configurable]), Security Deposit 
([Configurable]). All fee amounts are system-populated from the M-01 Configuration Console 
and require no code change to update. Approval hierarchy: DO (Yard Officer) → DV (Asst. 
Secretary) → Dy. Secretary → Joint Secretary → Secretary (DA) → Chairman (as per 
GAPLMB/10/INSP-YYYY/ inspection reports).

19.7 Appendix G — Traceability Items 
This appendix consolidates all Requirements Traceability Matrix (RTM) items. Status = 
Open indicates the corresponding test case has not yet been created or executed; this is 
expected at initial release and will be updated as development and testing progress. Items 
are grouped by module. Each requirement identifier links directly to the relevant module 
section. No FR with Priority = Critical may be signed off at UAT entry while its status 
remains Open. High and Medium items may be deferred to Regression testing at 
GAPLMB's written discretion. See Appendix C (RTM) for the full traceability matrix and 
test-case specification requirements.

Pre-Development Implementation Checklist 
The following decisions from Section 18 (Design Decisions) require implementation 
actions before UAT: 
Item 10 (M-03 Rent): TDS on rent: threshold implementation confirmed. Section 194-
I applies when annual rent exceeds ₹2,40,000. Configurable threshold must be 
implemented and validated before M-03 UAT sign-off. 
Item 12 (M-05 Receipts): Payment gateway selection: GAPLMB must formally select 
and communicate the chosen payment gateway (SBI ePay, NSDL, or RazorpayGov) 
to the development team prior to the M-05 build. Development cannot be finalised 
without this selection. 
Item 19 (M-06 Payments): Monthly Expenditure Statement submission deadline 
confirmed as the 6th of the following month. Advance Release is independent of the 
Expenditure Statement. Implementation must enforce the 6th deadline and the 
independence rule. 

--- PAGE 395 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 395 of 435 
19.8 Appendix H — Common Fields and Validation Rules 
 
This appendix consolidates all fields that appear across two or more modules of the GAPLMB 
Integrated Online Management System (IOMS). For each field, the following are documented: 
the field data type and size, the modules in which it is used, the existing validation rules as 
specified in the relevant module sections, proposed improvements to enhance usability, 
accuracy, and consistency, and recommended error messages for each field to ensure clarity for 
end-users at the point of failure. 
 
Legend  
 Mandatory: field must be filled before record submission.   
Conditional: field is mandatory only under specified conditions.   
Auto: field is system-generated; user input not required.

SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 434 of 435 
H.3 Cross-Cutting Non-Functional Requirements (Global UI and Validation 
Standards) 
 
The following requirements are mandatory globally across all modules and are not field-
specific. These shall be treated as binding NFRs and incorporated into the development 
standards, UI framework specifications, and acceptance test criteria. 
Area Mandatory Requirement 
1. Consistent Date Format Standardise all date inputs and displays to DD/MM/YYYY 
throughout the system. Enforce this via a unified date-picker 
component. Never display or accept dates in MM/DD/YYYY 
or YYYY-MM-DD format in any user-facing screen. 
2. Mandatory Field 
Indicators 
All mandatory fields must display a red asterisk (*) 
consistently. Optional fields should display (optional) in 
lighter font below the label. Conditional fields should 
dynamically show or hide the mandatory indicator based on 
the current context. 
3. Inline Validation on Blur Validate each field when the user moves focus away (on 
blur), not only on form submission. Display inline error 
messages directly below the field in red text. Do not wait 
until the user attempts to submit the form to reveal all errors. 
4. Confirmation on 
Irreversible Actions 
All irreversible or high-impact actions (DA approval, 
cancellation, status change to Demolished, submission of 
Monthly Returns) must display a confirmation dialog 
summarising the action and its consequences before 
execution. 
5. Auto-Save Drafts For long forms (Employee Master, Entity Master, Premises 
Allocation), implement auto-save of draft data every 5 
minutes. Display a Draft saved at HH:MM indicator. Drafts 
must be accessible only to the creating officer and cleared 

--- PAGE 435 ---
SRS for Integrated Online Management System GAPLMB • Confidential Page 435 of 435 
upon DA approval. 
6. Session Timeout 
Protection 
Warn users 5 minutes before their session expires with an 
Extend Session prompt. If the session expires mid-form, save 
a recoverable draft automatically so the user does not lose 
entered data. 
7. Audit Trail Visibility Every record in every module must display a read-only 
Activity Log panel showing all state changes with: timestamp 
(IST), actor name, role, action taken, and remarks (if any). 
This log must be accessible to the Auditor role at all times. 
8. Error Message 
Consistency 
All error messages must follow the format: [What went 
wrong] + [Why it happened] + [What the user should do 
next]. Avoid technical jargon, database error codes, or 
generic messages such as An error occurred. Each module's 
error messages must be catalogued in Appendix B. 
9. Mobile-First Input On mobile devices: date pickers must use the native mobile 
date-picker. Numeric fields must trigger the numeric keypad. 
Dropdowns must use the native mobile select or a full-screen 
modal. All touch targets must be at least 44x44 px. 
10. Duplicate Detection 
Before Submission 
For critical unique fields (PAN, GSTIN, Mobile No., Email, 
Employee ID), perform a server-side uniqueness check as 
soon as the field loses focus -- not only at form submission. 
Display a non-blocking warning with the conflicting record 
reference so the operator can investigate before completing 
the form.
